CREATE TABLE `recipe_ar` (
  `id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `recipe_id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `date` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci NOT NULL,
  `slugTitle` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `image` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `cookingTime` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `description` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `served` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `cat_id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `cat_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `cat_sub_titile` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `seo_page_title` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `seo_metadescription` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `seo_headline` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `directions` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `ingredients` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_swedish_ci NOT NULL,
  `status` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0'
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
